msg:The hotel is in the hutong. Once you walk in, the hustle and bustle is gone. There are shade trees and wind blowing, just like going back to childhood. There is a Huimin supermarket and a small restaurant inside. You can also meet uncles chatting in the hutong when you take a walk at night. It is especially suitable for friends who want to experience the hutong. Just be careful when taking a taxi, the hutong is very narrow and it is not easy to miss the car. There is an Overseas Chinese Museum at one end of the hutong, and the hotel has a voucher for the museum. The other end is connected to a bustling commercial street with all kinds of snacks. It is very close to the Confucius Temple, the Imperial College Museum, and the Lama Temple, and you can walk there. It takes only 10 minutes by car to the Sanlian Bookstore headquarters. You can experience beading in the hotel, there are food delivery robots, smart toilets, and a laundry room on the first floor, which is particularly good. The service is also very good. In short, it is a very good choice to use this hotel as a foothold to experience Beijing culture.
